<review>First the positives: this is a beautiful, modern property with views of Stag's Leap. The cabs from Cade and Odette are very good. The downsides: this is a completely corporate experience. We visited with fiends who are long time members of Cade. They would have a comped tasting but it was clear from the many signs that no other tasting would be comped. This is a big departure from most higher end wineries that want members to bring guests. Our guide came over and proceeded to talk extremely quickly through all 5 wines before departing to sit down with other guests. This is again a major departure from other "private" tastings. Finally we asked to compare the wines poured to others in their menu and we're told this wasn't possible. Overall, the experience was our worst in Napa and Sonoma in the past 5 years (multiple visits) just because of the retail atmosphere. We won't visit Cade, Odette, or Plumpjack again. <Review>I love this park! Most rimes we fo we're the only ones there. The grounds are clean, nicely landscaped and well-kempt. Park is right across the road from railroad tracks and trains do pass by every few minutes so prepare to hear their noise. We've seen folks flying their drones from the parking lot and there are tennis, handball and basketball courts and an 18-hole disc (Frisbee) golf course... something for just about everyone. There's a paw park for your dogs to enjoy and a walking trail of sorts. Allergy sufferers BEWARE and take your Zyrtec, Claritin, Allegra or whatever: there are dandelions and there's so many of them it looks and feels like a pollen alien attack. Picnic tables and little cast iron bbq grills spread about but we haven't used them yet. Best time to enjoy during the summer months is early in the morning or in the evening because it gets HOT right around 11 am and unless you're one of those strange souls who enjoys playing in heat that feels like a crematorium you'll want to govern yourself accordingly. Signs are posted warning of snakes, coyotes and mountain lions but so far we've only seen one coyote... from a distance... on the walking trail... following a lady who was walking her little dog. ðŸ˜²<//Review>< pics>

< Review>
I worked with Sean on selecting the correct rear shocks for my 04 Tacoma 4x4.  Having Bilstein 6112 up front, I wanted to match it up to the 5100 series, however the rear is stock height.  Sean dove in and verified the lengths for each shock (4600, 5100, 5160) and gave me several options to run the 5100 if I really wanted to, with the 4600 being recommended as the shock to get for stock height application.  The 5160 series matches closely to the 4600 in terms of collapse, extension, travel, and was the 2nd option if I choose to drop the cash on it.  This was a tricky one since not many folks run these shocks on 1st gen Tacoma trucks, but Sean helped and replied quickly.  Much appreciated for all the info!  I'll be waiting patiently until the 5160's are back in stock to get them!< /Review>

<user>115380237639711250386< /user><Name>Michael Lewis< /Name>< date>
1467726183855</date>
<Rating>5</Rating>< Review>
Reviewing Toyotapro is kind of a boring thing for me. I've taken my 96 Tacoma there since I bought it over ten years ago for all service, including an engine replacement at 286,000 miles. I make an appointment, drop the truck off at the scheduled time, the excellent mechanics do the work I ask for, they carefully look over my truck to give me a heads upon things that look like they will need to be replaced in the future,  I pay the price that they estimated or sometimes a bit less, then I take my truck home.

Toyotapro doesn't nickel and dime me on extras. They don't have sales quotas so they don't try and get me to pay them them to fix things that ain't broke. Sometimes I've wanted them to replace parts that didn't need replacing yet and they've advised against it, but went ahead with the work when I persisted. They even give me advice on services that they don't provide because they have a great base of knowledge and care about their customers and their vehicles. When I've needed major repairs they've advised me on the pros and cons of possible solutions then let me make my decision with no pressure.

So this is a boring review only because there is nothing to complain about. Toyotapro is exactly what would result from me designing the auto repair shop that fills my needs.</Review>

< review>
Came here on a weeknight with a reservation but probably didn't need one because it wasn't super busy.

My friend & I started with the pork belly which was really good. Super rich but melted in your mouth like butter.

They didn't have a bourbon menu, our waitress said they were working on it, but she recommended a whiskey she liked which ended up being delicious.

For our main course we both had the steak & frites (comes with bone marrow). I had mine rare and my friend had it medium rare. I didn't see too much of a difference between the way it was cooked but it leaned more toward the rare side which I didn't mind. The steak was fantastic, cooked & seasoned to perfection. The bone marrow was great, I dipped my fries in it.

Over all we had a great experience. The food was great, the price wasn't crazy and the service was very friendly and knowledgeable. I definitely recommend this place and will come back. :)</review>

<Review>The food at Bourbon and Beef is underwhelming, especially for the price, and the lackluster service doesn't do much to salvage the situation; I won't be going back.

We got a table right away on a not very busy Monday, placed our order, and then waited 30 minutes for soup and a salad to arrive. The server apologetically informed us that their computer crashed and the kitchen never got the order, but it shouldn't take 30 minutes for a server to realize there's a problem, especially when nearby tables that were seated after us were already getting food. Once the food arrived the mixed green salad and french onion soup were fine, but everything else was subpar. The burger was laughably tall, and even if it had been short enough to take a bite it fell apart instantly. The ravioli was fairly bland for $5 a piece, and the fingerling potatoes weren't the least bit crispy.

Overall, Bourbon and Beef was a waste of time and money, and almost anywhere else along College would be a better choice.< /Review>< rating>

< Review>
Made a reservation for 11:30 which I glad I made because this place was getting full. We started off with a couple of Morning Margaritas and ordered the steak and eggs and duck and waffles.

I wondered why they would call it a Morning Margarita then I took a sip. It was a strong punch of alcohol and bitterness from whatever citrus they added, probably lime; for $11 each it was worth it. Our food came and I have to say I had one of the best steaks of my life. With the steak and eggs came with potatoes and this sauce. The steak by itself was tender, seasoned very well, and the fat attached on the side really heightened the flavor all together. I guess that happens when itâ€™s grass-fed steak. The potatoes where cooked as perfectly as the steak, crispy on the outside and soft in the inside. Eggs were eggs and really there wasn't anything distinct.

I tried the duck from the duck and waffles and I have to say as someone who avoids duck because of the fear of tasting the gamy taste of duck this duck did not have it what-so-ever. It was delicious with the combination of the egg yolk and syrup. It did come with an orange jam which was very sweet and he used a little. For each entrÃ©e pricing at $17 (duck) and $20 (steak) so for the quality and taste of it, it was worth it.

Everything was going very well until I noticed a couple of the waitresses and a chef, the head maybe, where heavily discussing something because the looks on everyoneâ€™s faces did not look calm. <review>I was coming to the studio one morning from the city and my left front tire started to go.

George Oren Tire was able to fit me in within the second wave of business and I had to wait less time than I would at another tire service (Except for Boris - but that is another story) and the same amount of time I would wait at at oil change service.  Pretty performing.

Plus, the manager was able to evaluate and recommend quickly and cost effectively.  My service began shortly thereafter following a pleasant conversation with another customer who bragged she'd been bringing all her vehicles there forever.

But before I let the sparkle get the dazzle in my eyes, I waited to see how things went.  My tire needed plugging and they found another that needed plugging that I didn't even know about while performing inspection.

The manager told me that because he had already quoted me one price for the first plug, he wasn't going to charge me for the second one.  He said he was not a pump and dumper, and I laughed with him.

Things went great and he did a free rotation included.  It has been running well since, but my experience working in service stations taught me not to rely on plugged tires so much as new ones, and Oren management advised rightly so while simultaneously estimating two good new tires for the maintenance of my vehicle.

About three weeks later when I was looking for the money to grab two new tires where the plugged ones were running, I got a 20% discount coupon on service which would have brought me to less than 100 dollars each for the new tires installed.

Unfortunately, I couldn't catch that wave, but I bet he will honor the offer if I brings in the June expiring coupon sometime this July.

Even if he doesn't I recommend their service to everyone and rate highest my own experience with George Oren Tire Specialist.

The LC

UPDATE: 7/14/2018:

Glad to hear my coupon is still valid and I look forward to conducting business soon.

I wanted to share the experience I just had with Memorial Care Imaging, both the Newport Beach and Huntington Beach offices. I was scheduled this morning for an ultrasound at 8:30am, and unfortunately I received a call from a representative at the Newport Beach office that their ultrasound machine was not working. Instead of just scheduling me for the next time that their machine would be functioning, the representative, whom I apologize for not remembering her name, made the effort to reschedule me for just under (3) hours later at the Huntington Beach office. Upon arrival, I was immediately greeted by a young man who checked me in (again, I apologize for not remembering his name). He was very professional, attentive, and helped make me feel comfortable. He was not only that way with me, but also with other patients who checked in thereafter. Nicole, the technician who conducted the ultrasound, was just wonderful. She was also very professional, attentive to my concerns, and very trusting from the moment she called me and took me back to the examination room. I just left their office, and I will say that this was one of the best experiences I have ever had. Thanks to everyone at both the Newport Beach and Huntington Beach offices for making patients like myself feel comfortable.< /text>

< review>
Memorial Care is great. The Imaging Center is in a brand new buildings. There is plenty of free parking. The staff were awesome! Scheduling the appointment was easy and they got me in right away. Josh called me the night before to confirm and to give me important information about the appointment. Josh was also there in the morning to greet me. He is very friendly and efficient. When it came time for the MRI I was a little stressed out because I am claustrophobic. Aja who performed the procedure was fantastic. She put me at ease. She was very friendly and personable. She explained the procedure which helped me relax by knowing what to expect. She explained that it is a newer machine and that the new machine was a little wider so I didn't feel as confined. She put some headphones on me and played Pink Floyd Dark Side of the Moon for me. Next thing you know it was over. Have no fears about using this place. It is a first class operation.</review>
